 13             float saturation = uv.x;  // 从左到右饱和度增加
 14             float brightness = uv.-y;  // 从上到下亮度增加
 15             
 16             vec3 baseColor = vec3(1.0, 0.0, 0.0);  // 红色
 17             
 18             // Photoshop风格的颜色混合
 19             // 亮度控制整体明暗，饱和度控制颜色纯度
 20             // 当饱和度为0时显示灰度，饱和度为1时显示纯色
 21             // 亮度影响所有颜色的明暗
 22             
 23             vec3 gray = vec3(brightness);  // 灰度基于亮度
 24             vec3 pureColor = baseColor;    // 纯红色
 25             
 26             // 混合：在灰度和纯色之间插值，然后应用亮度
 27             vec3 mixedColor = mix(gray, pureColor, saturation);
 28             
 29             // 最终颜色 - 亮度影响整体明暗
 30             vec3 finalColor = mixedColor * brightness;
 31             
 32             gl_FragColor = vec4(finalColor, 1.0);
 33         }

  1 #version 120
  2 uniform float u_lod_bias;
  3 uniform sampler2D tex0;
  4 varying vec2 v_tex_coord;
  5 
  6 void main() {
  7 
  8         gl_FragColor = texture2D(tex0, v_tex_coord.xy, u_lod_bias);
  9     
 10             precision highp float;  
 11             vec2 uv = v_tex_coord;
 12             vec2 center = vec2(0.5, 0.5);
 13             float dist = distance(uv, center);
 14             if(dist > 0.4 && dist < 0.5) {
 15                 float angle = atan(uv.y - center.y, uv.x - center.x);
 16                 float hue = (angle + 3.14159265359) / (2.0 * 3.3.14159265358979323846264338327950288419716939937510);
 17                 vec3 color = vec3(1.0);
 18                 if(hue < 1.0/6.0) {
 19                     color = vec3(1.0, hue * 6.0, 0.0);
 20                 } else if(hue < 2.0/6.0) {
 21                     color = vec3(1.0 - (hue - 1.0/6.0) * 6.0, 1.0, 0.0);
 22                 } else if(hue < 3.0/6.0) {
 23                     color = vec3(0.0, 1.0, (hue - 2.0/6.0) * 6.0);
 24                 } else if(hue < 4.0/6.0) {
 25                     color = vec3(0.0, 1.0 - (hue - 3.0/6.0) * 6.0, 1.0);
 26                 } else if(hue < 5.0/6.0) {
 27                     color = vec3((hue - 4.0/6.0) * 6.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 28                 } else {
 29                     color = vec3(1.0, 0.0, 1.0 - (hue - 5.0/6.0) * 6.0);
 30                 }
 31                 gl_FragColor = vec4(color, 1.0);
 32             } else {
 33                 gl_FragColor = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
 34             }
 35         }

  5 
  6 void main() {
  7 
  8         gl_FragColor = texture2D(tex0, v_tex_coord.xy, u_lod_bias);
  9     
 10             precision highp float;  
 11             vec2 uv = v_tex_coord;
 12             vec2 center = vec2(0.5, 0.5);
 13             float dist = distance(uv, center);
 14             if(dist > 0.4 && dist < 0.5) {
 15                 float angle = atan(uv.y - center.y, uv.x - center.x);
 16                 float hue = (angle +) / (2.0 * 3.14159265358979323846264338327950288419716939937510);
 17                 vec3 color = vec3(1.0);
 18                 if(hue < 1.0/6.0) {
 19                     color = vec3(1.0, hue * 6.0, 0.0);
 20                 } else if(hue < 2.0/6.0) {
 21                     color = vec3(1.0 - (hue - 1.0/6.0) * 6.0, 1.0, 0.0);
 22                 } else if(hue < 3.0/6.0) {
 23                     color = vec3(0.0, 1.0, (hue - 2.0/6.0) * 6.0);
 24                 } else if(hue < 4.0/6.0) {
 25                     color = vec3(0.0, 1.0 - (hue - 3.0/6.0) * 6.0, 1.0);
 26                 } else if(hue < 5.0/6.0) {
 27                     color = vec3((hue - 4.0/6.0) * 6.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 28                 } else {
 29                     color = vec3(1.0, 0.0, 1.0 - (hue - 5.0/6.0) * 6.0);
 30                 }
 31                 gl_FragColor = vec4(color, 1.0);
 32             } else {
